<h1>A Novel Framework for Spatiotemporal Monitoring and Post-Signal Diagnosis of Processes with Image Data</h1>
<p align='center'>Farzad Amirkhani, Amirhossein Amiri</p>
<h2 id="introduction">Introduction</h2>
<p>
The spread of emerging technologies and advances in measuring devices has led to an increase in the amount of data obtained from manufacturing systems in recent years. For instance, the use of sensors and machine vision systems in the manufacturing companies has led to a massive amount of data, which extracting information from this data and exploiting them effectively is one of the most fundamental challenges of data science and statistical process monitoring.
The codes in this repository are presented to monitor image data and post-signal diagnostic procedures (change point estimation and fault location identification) which are related to the paper entitled <strong>A Novel Framework for Spatiotemporal Monitoring and Post-Signal Diagnosis of Processes with Image Data</strong>. </p>
<h2 id="codes">Codes</h2>
<p >After removing the background, the obtained image <strong>Tile_250.jpg</strong> is considered as the nominal image. In simulation studies, single, multiple and circular faults are imposed at a specific location of the image and  performance of the proposed method is evaluated for which this repository including three .m files namely <strong>SingleFault.m</strong>, <strong>MultiFault.m</strong>, and <strong>CircularFault.m</strong> is provided. The first six line of these files are the same as below:
<pre><code>clc;
clear;
I=double(rgb2gray(imread('Tile_250.jpg')));
[m,n]=size(I);
changePoint=5;
Delta=[-10:-1,1:10];</code></pre> 
<p> In the above mentioned codes, after initialization, which includes <code>clc</code> and <code>clear</code> commands, the image entitled <code>Tile_250.jpg</code> is read and converted from RGB to grayscale form, and saved as matrix <code>I</code>, then its dimensions are saved as <code>m</code> and <code>n</code> variables. In the next line, the change point is set equal to 5 for all simulation runs. Shifts in intensity values are considered as <code>Delta</code> vector in the ranges of [-10,-1] and [1,10] and defined in line six of the above code.</p> 
<h3 >The SingleFault.m file</h3>
<p>This .m file is used to generate a fault with specific dimensions at the specific location of the image. The location of the fault is determined in the image with its coordinates, which are <code>X1</code>, <code>X2</code>, <code>Y1</code>, and <code>Y2</code>.

The best case and worst case scenarios are generated based on the values of <code>X1</code>, <code>X2</code>, <code>Y1</code>, and <code>Y2</code>. Shifts are imposed to <code>De</code> matrix, which is created based on the <code>I</code> matrix and used to simulate defective images. <code>Idn</code> matrix is defined to calculate similarity dice index in the next parts of the code which is a matrix that defective locations take 1, and the other locations take 0 in it.   
The function <strong>SMPSD</strong> at the next line gets the <code>I</code>, <code>De</code>, <code>Idn</code>, and <code>changepoint</code> values and returns <code>Result</code> value. The next lines of code are written to save <code>Result</code> as .mat files in the workspace with the name of <strong>filename</strong>. This procedure is performed for the best and worst cases with different sizes of fault as below (The results of each part of code is reported after it).</p>
<pre><code>%% The best-case scenario with a 5×5 fault size (Table 2)
X1=1;X2=5;
Y1=1;Y2=5;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Single','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X1),'_',num2str(X2),...
        '_',num2str(Y1),'_',num2str(Y2),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

5px;border-style:solid;border-width:1px;overflow:hidden;word-break:keep-all;border-color:black;text-align:left;vertical-align:center">0.03</td></tr></table><pre><code>%% The best-case scenario with a 10×10 fault size (Table 3)
X1=1;X2=10;
Y1=1;Y2=10;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Single','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X1),'_',num2str(X2),...
        '_',num2str(Y1),'_',num2str(Y2),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<pre><code>%% The best-case scenario with a 15×15 fault size (Table 4)
X1=1;X2=15;
Y1=1;Y2=15;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Single','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X1),'_',num2str(X2),...
        '_',num2str(Y1),'_',num2str(Y2),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

5px;border-style:solid;border-width:1px;overflow:hidden;word-break:keep-all;border-color:black;text-align:left;vertical-align:center">0.01</td></tr></table><pre><code>%% The worst-case scenario with a 5×5 fault size (Table 5)
X1=3;X2=7;
Y1=3;Y2=7;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Single','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X1),'_',num2str(X2),...
        '_',num2str(Y1),'_',num2str(Y2),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<pre><code>%% The worst-case scenario with a 10×10 fault size (Table 6)
X1=3;X2=12;
Y1=3;Y2=12;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Single','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X1),'_',num2str(X2),...
        '_',num2str(Y1),'_',num2str(Y2),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<pre><code> %% The worst-case scenario with a 15×15 fault size (Table 7)
X1=3;X2=17;
Y1=3;Y2=17;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=De(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X1:X2,Y1:Y2)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Single','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X1),'_',num2str(X2),...
        '_',num2str(Y1),'_',num2str(Y2),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<h3 >The MultiFault.m file</h3> <p>This code is similar to SingleFault.m. The only difference is that in this code, instead of creating single fault, two faults are imposed to the image in different locations, such that there are  <code>X11</code>, <code>X12</code>, <code>Y11</code>, and <code>Y12</code> for the first fault, and  <code>X21</code>, <code>X22</code>, <code>Y21</code>, and <code>Y22</code> for the second one (The results of each part of code is reported after it).</p>

<pre><code>clc;
clear;
I=double(rgb2gray(imread('Tile_250.jpg')));
[m,n]=size(I);
changePoint=5;
Delta=[-10:-1,1:10];
%% The best-case scenario with two 5×5 fault size (Table 8)
X11=1; X12=5;
Y11=1; Y12=5;
X21=246; X22=250;
Y21=246; Y22=250;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)+Delta(i);
    De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=1;
    Idn(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Multi','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X11),'_',num2str(X12),...
        '_',num2str(Y11),'_',num2str(Y12)','_',num2str(X21),'_',num2str(X22),...
        '_',num2str(Y21),'_',num2str(Y22),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<pre><code>%% The best-case scenario with two 10×10 fault size (Table 9)
X11=1; X12=10;
Y11=1; Y12=10;
X21=241; X22=250;
Y21=241; Y22=250;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)+Delta(i);
    De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=1;
    Idn(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Multi','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X11),'_',num2str(X12),...
        '_',num2str(Y11),'_',num2str(Y12)','_',num2str(X21),'_',num2str(X22),...
        '_',num2str(Y21),'_',num2str(Y22),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<pre><code>%% The best-case scenario with two 15×15 fault size (Table 10)
X11=1; X12=15;
Y11=1; Y12=15;
X21=236; X22=250;
Y21=236; Y22=250;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)+Delta(i);
    De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=1;
    Idn(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Multi','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X11),'_',num2str(X12),...
        '_',num2str(Y11),'_',num2str(Y12)','_',num2str(X21),'_',num2str(X22),...
        '_',num2str(Y21),'_',num2str(Y22),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<pre><code>%% The worst-case scenario with two 5×5 fault size (Table 11)
X11=3; X12=7;
Y11=3; Y12=7;
X21=243; X22=247;
Y21=243; Y22=247;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)+Delta(i);
    De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=1;
    Idn(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Multi','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X11),'_',num2str(X12),...
        '_',num2str(Y11),'_',num2str(Y12)','_',num2str(X21),'_',num2str(X22),...
        '_',num2str(Y21),'_',num2str(Y22),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<pre><code>%% The worst-case scenario with two 10×10 fault size (Table 12)
X11=3; X12=12;
Y11=3; Y12=12;
X21=238; X22=247;
Y21=238; Y22=247;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)+Delta(i);
    De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=1;
    Idn(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Multi','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X11),'_',num2str(X12),...
        '_',num2str(Y11),'_',num2str(Y12)','_',num2str(X21),'_',num2str(X22),...
        '_',num2str(Y21),'_',num2str(Y22),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

5px;border-style:solid;border-width:1px;overflow:hidden;word-break:keep-all;border-color:black;text-align:center;vertical-align:center" colspan="11">Results for the worst-case scenario including two <pre><code>%% The worst-case scenario with two 15×15 fault size (Table 13)
X11=3; X12=17;
Y11=3; Y12=17;
X21=233; X22=247;
Y21=233; Y22=247;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=De(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)+Delta(i);
    De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=De(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)+Delta(i);
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    Idn(X11:X12,Y11:Y12)=1;
    Idn(X21:X22,Y21:Y22)=1;
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Multi','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(X11),'_',num2str(X12),...
        '_',num2str(Y11),'_',num2str(Y12)','_',num2str(X21),'_',num2str(X22),...
        '_',num2str(Y21),'_',num2str(Y22),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<h3 >The CircularFault.m file</h3>
<p>In this .m file, a circular fault with center point of <code>(CX,CY)</code>, and radius of <code>R</code> is imposed to image based on circle equation with different radius (The results of each part of code is reported after it).
<pre><code>clc;
clear;
I=double(rgb2gray(imread('Tile_250.jpg')));
[m,n]=size(I);
changePoint=5;
Delta=[-10:-1,1:10];
%% Circular fault with a radius of 5 (Table 14)
R=5;
CX=50;CY=50;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    for ii=1:m
        for jj=1:n
            if ((ii-CX)^2+(jj-CY)^2<=(R^2))
                De(ii,jj)=De(ii,jj)+Delta(i);
                Idn(ii,jj)=1;
            end
        end
    end
    
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Circular','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(CX),'_',num2str(CY),...
        '_',num2str(R),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<pre><code>%% Circular fault with a radius of 10 (Table 15)
R=10;
CX=50;CY=50;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    for ii=1:m
        for jj=1:n
            if ((ii-CX)^2+(jj-CY)^2<=(R^2))
                De(ii,jj)=De(ii,jj)+Delta(i);
                Idn(ii,jj)=1;
            end
        end
    end
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Circular','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(CX),'_',num2str(CY),...
        '_',num2str(R),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end
</code></pre>

style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;padding:1px sans-serif;font-size:14px;padding:1px 5px;border-style:solid;border-width:1px;overflow:hidden;word-break:keep-all;border-color:black;text-align:left;vertical-align:center">0.01</td></tr></table>

<pre><code>%% Circular fault with a radius of 15 (Table 16)
R=15;
CX=50;CY=50;
for i=1:numel(Delta)
    De=I;
    Idn=zeros(m,n);
    for ii=1:m
        for jj=1:n
            if ((ii-CX)^2+(jj-CY)^2<=(R^2))
                De(ii,jj)=De(ii,jj)+Delta(i);
                Idn(ii,jj)=1;
            end
        end
    end
    
    Result=SMPSD(I,De,Idn,changePoint)
    filename=['Result-Circular','(',num2str(Delta(i)),')_',num2str(CX),'_',num2str(CY),...
        '_',num2str(R),'.mat']
    save(filename,'Result')
end</code></pre>

<h3 align="justify" >The SMPSD file</h3>
<p align="justify">This function gets the <code>I</code>,<code>De</code>,<code>Idn</code>, and <code>changePoint</code> values and returns performance measures as<code>Result</code> variable as below:</p>

<pre><code><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">Result</span>=<span class="hljs-title">SMPSD</span><span class="hljs-params">(I,De,Idn,changePoint)</span></span>
</code></pre>

<p align="justify">Two loops are needed to calculate average run length (<strong>ARL</strong>), the inner loop calculates the run length based on simulation for one iteration, and the outer loop repeats the inner loop based on the value of <code>Maxit</code> to calculate the performance measures. At each outer loop the value of <code>t</code> is set equal to 1, and <code>flag</code> is set equal to true.</p>

<pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Maxit</span>=<span class="hljs-number">2000</span><span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
<span class="hljs-attribute">it</span>=<span class="hljs-number">1</span><span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
while it&lt;=Maxit
    t=<span class="hljs-number">1</span><span class="hljs-comment">;flag=true;</span>
    while flag
</code></pre>

<p align="justify">At the next lines of the code, the <code>Error</code> matrix is generated based on <strong>Simulator</strong> function. The <code>Error</code> matrix with dimension of 250 * 250 is separated to 5 * 5 square regions and then converted to 1 * 25 vectors with <strong>Separator</strong> function to be used in ANOVA.
The control level is also created to be compared with regions in the image based on Dunnett&#39;s test.</p>

<pre><code>        Error{<span class="hljs-built_in">t</span>}=zeros(<span class="hljs-number">250</span>,<span class="hljs-number">250</span>);
        Error{<span class="hljs-built_in">t</span>}=Simulator(I,changePoint,De,<span class="hljs-built_in">t</span>);
        TR=Separator(Error{<span class="hljs-built_in">t</span>});
        TR(<span class="hljs-symbol">:</span>,<span class="hljs-number">2501</span>)=normrnd(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>,<span class="hljs-number">2.55</span>,[<span class="hljs-number">25</span>,<span class="hljs-number">1</span>]);
</code></pre>

<p align="justify">In the following lines, ANOVA is applied to <code>TR</code> values. Three conditions are possible to happen based on the p-value result:</p>
<ol align="justify">
<li>if p-value&gt;.005, the process is in control, so <code>flag</code> is set equal to true and run length is added by 1.</li>

<li>if p&lt;.005, and t&lt;changePoint, a false alarm is given and the last iteration in inner loop must be repeated.</li>

<li><p>if p&lt;.005, and t&gt;changePoint, the process is out of control. In such a case, run length of the iteration is saved as <code>RL(it)</code> and post-signal diagnosis of process is applied on data. At the end, the <code>it</code> value is added by 1 and the inner loop is terminated by <code>break</code>.</p>

<pre><code>     [p,tbl,stats]=anova1(TR,[],<span class="hljs-string">'off'</span>)<span class="hljs-comment">;</span>

     <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> p&gt;<span class="hljs-number">.005</span>
         flag=<span class="hljs-literal">true</span><span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
         t=t+<span class="hljs-number">1</span><span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
     <span class="hljs-keyword">elseif</span> p&lt;<span class="hljs-number">.005</span> &amp;&amp; t&lt;=changePoint
         t=t<span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
         flag=<span class="hljs-literal">true</span><span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
     <span class="hljs-keyword">elseif</span> p&lt;<span class="hljs-number">.005</span> &amp;&amp; t&gt;changePoint
         RL(it)
</code></pre>
<p align="justify">In order to identify the location of the fault in the image, Dunnet&#39;s test is utilized. For this aim, the <strong>Dunnett.m</strong> file written by <strong>Navin Pokala</strong> is used which is available <a href="https://www.mathworks.com/matlabcentral/fileexchange/38157-dunnett-m/">here</a>. Then, the regions which are detected as defective locations are stored as <code>Region</code>. In the case that the <code>Region</code> variable was empty, the Region with minimum p-value is considered as defective location in the image.</p>

<pre><code>            p_Dunnet = dunnett(stats,[],<span class="hljs-number">2501</span>);
            Region=<span class="hljs-built_in">find</span>(p_Dunnet(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:<span class="hljs-number">2500</span>)&lt;<span class="hljs-number">.005</span>);
            <span class="hljs-built_in">if</span>  isempty(Region)
                [~,Region]=<span class="hljs-built_in">min</span>(p_Dunnet(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:<span class="hljs-number">2500</span>));
            <span class="hljs-built_in">end</span>
</code></pre>

<p align="justify">The <strong>Jointer</strong> function reshapes the <code>Region</code> variable to a 250*250 matrix, that is <code>Est250</code>.</p>

<pre><code>            Est250=Jointer(<span class="hljs-name">Region</span>)<span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
</code></pre>

<p align="justify">The change point of process is estimated based on MLE method, as below:</p>

<pre><code>            <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> tt=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:RL(<span class="hljs-keyword">it</span>)
                FF=find(Est250==<span class="hljs-number">1</span>);
                Xbar(tt)=mean(Error{tt}(FF));
            <span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
            TTT=<span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
            f=[];
            <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> tow=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:RL(<span class="hljs-keyword">it</span>)
                XBarBar(tow)=(sum(Xbar(TTT+<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:<span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>)))/(RL(<span class="hljs-keyword">it</span>)-TTT);
                f(tow)=(RL(<span class="hljs-keyword">it</span>)-TTT)*((XBarBar(tow)<span class="hljs-number">-0</span>)^<span class="hljs-number">2</span>);
                TTT=TTT+<span class="hljs-number">1</span>;
            <span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
            [~,Ch(<span class="hljs-keyword">it</span>)]=max(f);
            Ch(<span class="hljs-keyword">it</span>)=Ch(<span class="hljs-keyword">it</span>)<span class="hljs-number">-6</span>;
</code></pre>

<p align="justify">At the last part of code, the performance measures such as ARL, the difference between real and the estimated change point, and Sørensen–Dice coefficient are calculated and saved in the <code>Result</code> variable.</p>
<pre><code>            dice(it) = <span class="hljs-number">2</span>*nnz(Idn&amp;Est250)/(nnz(Est250) + nnz(Idn))<span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
            <span class="hljs-keyword">clc</span><span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
            fprintf(<span class="hljs-string">'The Current ARL = %6.4f,changepoint=%6.4f,SDCS=%6.4f, after %d simulations when delta =%6.4f'</span>,mean(RL)-<span class="hljs-number">5</span>,mean(<span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>),mean(dice),it,Delta)<span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
            it=it+<span class="hljs-number">1</span><span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
        end
    end 
end

Result=[mean(RL)-changePoint
    <span class="hljs-keyword">std</span>(RL) median(<span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>) mean(<span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">std</span>(<span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>) numel(find(<span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>==<span class="hljs-number">0</span>))/Maxit (numel(find(<span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>&lt;=<span class="hljs-number">2</span> &amp;<span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>&gt;<span class="hljs-number">0</span> ))+numel(find(<span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>&gt;=-<span class="hljs-number">2</span> &amp; <span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-number">0</span> )))/Maxit  ...
    numel(find(<span class="hljs-number">Ch</span>&gt;<span class="hljs-number">2</span>))/Maxit mean(dice) <span class="hljs-keyword">std</span>(dice)]<span class="hljs-comment">;</span>
</code></pre>

<h3>The Simulator.mat file</h3>
<p align="justify">This function gets intensity values of nominal image (<code>I</code>), intensity values of image with fault (<code>De</code>), <code>change point</code> and <code>t</code> and generates the <code>Error</code> matrix as a result.</p>

<pre><code><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">Error</span>=<span class="hljs-title">Simulator</span><span class="hljs-params">(I,changePoint,De,t)</span>
[<span class="hljs-title">m</span>,<span class="hljs-title">n</span>]=<span class="hljs-title">size</span><span class="hljs-params">(I)</span>;</span>
WN=normrnd(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>,<span class="hljs-number">2.55</span>,[m,n]);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> t&lt;=changePoint
        Sim=I+WN;
            <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>
        Sim=De+WN;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
Error=Sim-I;
<span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
</code></pre>

<h3 align="justify">The Separator.mat file</h3>
<p>The purpose of using this .m file is to separate the image into 5 * 5 squares and then convert them into vectors. It gets <code>Error</code> matrix as input and gives <code>TR</code> matrix as a result.</p>

<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> TR=Separator(Error)
    [m,n]=size(Error);
    k=<span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ii=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:(m/<span class="hljs-number">5</span>)
            <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> jj=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:(n/<span class="hljs-number">5</span>)
                k=k+<span class="hljs-number">1</span>;
                Roi{ii,jj}=Error(<span class="hljs-number">5</span>*ii-<span class="hljs-number">4</span>:<span class="hljs-number">5</span>*ii,<span class="hljs-number">5</span>*jj-<span class="hljs-number">4</span>:<span class="hljs-number">5</span>*jj);
                TR<span class="hljs-comment">(:,k)=Roi{ii,jj}(:)</span>;
            <span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
</code></pre><h3 id="the-jointer-mat-file">The Jointer.mat file</h3>
<p>This code gets <code>Region</code> matrix as input and gives <code>Est250</code> matrix as a result.</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">Est250</span>=<span class="hljs-title">Jointer</span><span class="hljs-params">(Region)</span></span>
Est50=<span class="hljs-built_in">zeros</span>(<span class="hljs-number">50</span>,<span class="hljs-number">50</span>);
Est50(Region)=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>;
Est250=<span class="hljs-built_in">zeros</span>(<span class="hljs-number">250</span>,<span class="hljs-number">250</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ii=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:<span class="hljs-number">50</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> jj=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:<span class="hljs-number">50</span>
            Est250(<span class="hljs-number">5</span>*ii<span class="hljs-number">-4</span>:<span class="hljs-number">5</span>*ii,<span class="hljs-number">5</span>*jj<span class="hljs-number">-4</span>:<span class="hljs-number">5</span>*jj)=Est50(ii,jj);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">end</span>
</code></pre>
<p>For comprehensive information about this project please see the paper with the following link <a href="??">???</a>. </P>
